style="font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">______________________</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">COVINGTON, LA. (</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">July&#160;23, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">) </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#8211; Pool Corporation (NASDAQ/GSM:POOL) today reported record results for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#8220;Our domestic blue business realized 6% sales growth year to date and 3% sales growth in the second quarter of 2015 compared to the prior year periods.  Adverse weather conditions in a number of our significant markets affected our second quarter growth, as did the shift of early buy shipments into the first quarter.  Our customers currently have a larger than normal backlog, given lost workdays, as a result of record rainfall in many important markets.  Conversely, in markets where weather was normal, our results met or exceeded our expectations.  In local currencies, our international business generated an estimated 8% aggregate sales growth rate year to date and an estimated 6% aggregate sales growth rate for the quarter.  When translated into U.S. dollars, our international business negatively impacted our consolidated sales growth rates due to the nearly 20% appreciation of the U.S. dollar relative to most international currencies since this time last year,&#8221; said Manuel&#160;Perez&#160;de&#160;la&#160;Mesa, President and CEO.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Net sales for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;were a record </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$851.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$848.2 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#160;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, with base business sales flat for the period.  The decline in foreign currency exchange rates relative to the U.S. dollar negatively impacted our consolidated sales growth rate by approximately 2% period over period.  Excessive precipitation in Texas and adjacent states significantly impacted our second quarter sales, delaying construction projects and reducing spending on related discretionary products.  Cooler than normal temperatures in the Midwest and the Northeast delayed pool openings and inhibited sales growth in these markets.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Gross profit for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">1%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to a record </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$248.3 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;from </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$247.0 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the same period of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  Gross profit as a percentage of net sales (gross margin) was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">29.1%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in both the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Selling and administrative expenses (operating expenses) decreased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">4%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$119.1 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared to the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, with base business operating expenses down </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">6%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the period.  The stronger U.S. dollar relative to foreign currencies favorably impacted our operating expenses by approximately 2%.  A reduction in performance-based employee compensation also contributed to this decline.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Operating income for the quarter increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">5%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to a record </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$129.1 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared to the same period in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  Operating income as a percentage of net sales (operating margin) was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">15.2%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">14.4%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  The effect of foreign currency fluctuations from the strengthening of the U.S. dollar on consolidated operating income is an estimated $2.2 million, which includes the comparison of our foreign subsidiaries&#8217; second quarter 2015 local currency operating income translated at historical second quarter 2014 exchange rates, to their reported second quarter 2014 U.S. dollar operating income.</font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">1</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s2DB8515641935135851B8E9B85D70604"></a><br><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Net income attributable to Pool Corporation increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">5%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to a record </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$77.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#160;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$73.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.   Earnings per share was a record </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$1.75</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per diluted share for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">three months</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;versus </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$1.61</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per diluted share for the comparable period in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  We estimate a $0.03 negative impact on earnings per share in the quarter versus the comparable 2014 period, due to the impact of the stronger U.S. dollar on the translation of foreign currency denominated earnings. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Net sales for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">4%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to a record </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$1,302.3 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;from </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$1,254.6 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the comparable </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;period, with much of this growth coming from the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">3%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;improvement in base business sales.  There was a 2% negative foreign currency translation impact on our consolidated sales growth rate for the first half of 2015 compared to the first half of 2014.  Gross margin decreased approximately 15&#160;basis points to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">28.6%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the first half of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;from the same period last year. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Operating expenses declined </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">1%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared to the first half of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, with base business operating expenses down </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  The stronger U.S. dollar relative to foreign currencies favorably impacted our year to date operating expenses by approximately 2%.  Operating income for the first six months of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">10%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$144.7 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$131.1 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the same period last year.  Operating income was adversely affected by an estimated $1.9 million from the impact of foreign currency translation.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Earnings per share for the first six months of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">15%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to a record </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$1.94</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per diluted share on net income attributable to Pool Corporation of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$86.3 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$1.69</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per diluted share on net income of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$78.1 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the comparable </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;period.  We estimate a $0.03 negative impact on earnings per share versus the comparable 2014 period due to the impact of the stronger U.S. dollar on the translation of foreign currency denominated earnings.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">On the balance sheet, total net receivables and net inventory levels increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">4%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">5%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, respectively, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  Total debt outstanding at </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$495.3 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, up </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">15%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">June&#160;30, 2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Cash </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">used in</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;operations was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$56.6 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the first </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;months of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$50.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#160;for the first </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;months of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.  The increase in cash used is primarily related to our accounts receivable growth as well as timing differences in our accounts payable cycle.  Adjusted EBITDA (as defined in the addendum to this release) was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$135.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$128.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, respectively, and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$157.5 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$143.3 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the first </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;months of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, respectively.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#8220;With the first half of 2015 behind us, we are narrowing our annual earnings guidance range to $2.72 to $2.82 per diluted share, compared to our previous range of $2.72 to $2.87 per diluted share.  Achieving this would represent another year of solid earnings growth as we strive to provide exceptional value to our customers and suppliers.  It is in the heat of the season that our unprecedented investments make us THE source for industry professionals,&#8221; said Perez&#160;de&#160;la&#160;Mesa.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">POOLCORP is the world&#8217;s largest wholesale distributor of swimming pool and related backyard products.  Currently, POOLCORP operates </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">331</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;sales centers in North America, Europe, South America and Australia, through which it distributes more than 160,000 national brand and private label products to roughly 100,000 wholesale customers.  For more information, please visit www.poolcorp.com. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">This news release includes &#8220;forward-looking&#8221; statements that involve risk and uncertainties that are generally identifiable through the use of words such as &#8220;believe,&#8221; &#8220;expect,&#8221; &#8220;intend,&#8221; &#8220;plan,&#8221; &#8220;estimate,&#8221; &#8220;project,&#8221; &#8220;should&#8221;  and similar expressions and include projections of earnings. style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Adjusted EBITDA</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">We define Adjusted EBITDA as net income or net loss plus interest expense, income taxes, depreciation, amortization, share&#8209;based compensation, goodwill and other non-cash impairments and equity earnings or loss in unconsolidated investments.&#160;&#160;Adjusted EBITDA is not a measure of cash flow or liquidity as determined by generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP).  We have included Adjusted EBITDA as a supplemental disclosure because we believe that it is widely used by our investors, industry analysts and others as a useful supplemental liquidity measure in conjunction with cash flows provided by or used&#160;in operating activities to help investors understand our ability to provide cash flows to fund growth, service debt and pay dividends as well as compare our cash flow generating capacity from year to year.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">We believe Adjusted EBITDA should be considered in addition to, not as a substitute for, operating income or loss, net income or loss, cash flows provided by or used in operating, investing and financing activities or other income statement or cash flow statement line items reported in accordance with GAAP.  Other companies may calculate Adjusted EBITDA differently than we do, which may limit its usefulness as a comparative measure</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div
